<Name>Evelyn Barri< /Name>< Text>
BEWARE! I took dog in for exam prior to dental cleaning.  5 days later, in the middle of the night, he started coughing, hacking and spitting up white foam.  I called Banfield  and was told they were very busy and could not see him for 4 days.  I took him to another vet and found out he had kennel cough.

Obviously they exposed him to a sick dog.  Kennel cough is highly  contagious and you must keep sick dogs away from you healthy ones.  Dogs with kennel cough should be quarantined and kept away from healthy dogs.  The virus can be carried by those who have been around them so the vets, techs, etc.  need to change clothes, wash their hands and do all they can not to spread the disease

He was better in a matter of days.  It cost me $190.00 to get him treated but it was worth it because I now have a new vet who does not demand unnecessary tests, etc. just to hike up the bill.  The manager of Banfield said if I had brought him in they would have wanted X-rays, bloodwork etc.<//Text>

<Text>Took my very healthy cat in for vaccinations and a yearly exam.  He is a healthy, indoor only, domestic cat.  Active, playful, cuddly, and VERY healthy.  I told the vet I just wanted a yearly visit (but this doesn't meet their ideal customer if money only comes in once)!  She immediately told me he had a heart murmur and needs blood work done.  Without missing a beat she laid out a financial plan on the table for me to choose from.  Blood work will cost $200 plus the cost of vaccines and a visit -- now were talking almost $300...might as well take advantage of the plan at $25/month for a yearly contract.  This made sense to me so I signed up at that rate.  She took my cat into the backroom without me.  Separating animal from owner (look out for places like this you guys seriously)!  She ran blood work and came back with nothing.  She recommended we move forward with a urine analysis -- an additional cost that I can bring down for the low price of $35/month on the upgraded plan...I declined this and opted for a cheaper test --which also showed nothing.  Her next recommendation was an echo cardiogram of which costs $700!  Keep in mind, I brought in a healthy, active and very normal cat.  I told her that this was getting a bit ridiculous and I need to discuss with my husband before moving forward with anything.  She then went on to tell me that we could put him down and all costs would be closed out for us and we wouldn't have to make monthly payments.
So....just kill my cat?

I left worried about my cat (they know you love your animal and they will manipulate that).

My husband and I decided to take our cat to another vet for a second opinion.  Guess who DOES NOT HAVE A HEART ISSUE!!  Banfield lied and manipulated my family to cheat us out of our money at $25/month.  I have no respect for their practice.

The vet wanted to kill my cat to make money off of us.  This would have broken our hearts...but hey as long as their pockets are lined it doesn't matter to them.< /Text>< pics>

Diddy went in for just some vaccinations but I also had several other concerns as well I wanted to discuss. Diddy had the surgeries under Dr. Dean and through the day of surgery and the two weeks to follow during his healing she was so attentive, helpful and in the middle of the healing when he had developed a double ear infection (when it rains it pours!!) Allie asked if I needed help, I told her yes I am looking for an Ulta duo eyeliner, and Allie actually remembered the product & explained it is a seasonal item then she went on to see if she could find me the plum shade I fell in love with. <Review>My experience at the hair salon was sub-par.

The reason I decided to try the hair salon at Ulta was because I received via mail a coupon for a $30 cut and style for new guests. It said to book online by 4/19/2017. On Wednesday the 19th, I didn't have access to wifi, so I called and made an appointment over the phone. The woman I spoke to said there were no walk-ins available for that day, so I made one for 1 o'clock the next day (Thursday).

When I arrived Thursday at 1, there was no one at the salon counter. After waiting a few moments, I went in search of an employee. The store was nearly empty, so I found one immediately. She directed me to Cecilia, who was to be my stylist. Cecilia acknowledged me then promptly walked away with some guy she had been talking to. I continued to wait at the salon bar for an extra 5-10 minutes while various other employees asked me if I had an appointment and didn't seem to know where Cecilia had gone. This all happened while on my lunch break, so I was under a time constraint.

Strangely, it wasn't until 3:54 pm that same day that I received a text confirming my appointment at 1 pm. A miscommunication about appointments is  understandable, but I found Cecilia's behavior to be unprofessional.

Additionally, I was not very satisfied with the haircut she gave. I asked for layers and a trim - I said that I don't mind sacrificing a bit of length if it makes my ends look healthier. But after she was finished, I had to ask her to go over certain spots again, because there were still lots of noticeable split ends. She also didn't cut the hair framing my face at all until I specifically requested.

My hair also felt very dry after the blowout. I was curious about the products she used. She used Redken anti-frizz shampoo, which I don't feel was very appropriate for my hair type. I'm not sure what hairspray she used (she wasn't sure when I asked), but it didn't seem to have any heat protective elements. My hair felt damaged after the blowout.

And finally, she was very rough with the way she handled my hair. She neglected to brush out any of the tangles after washing my hair, so each time she made a long pass with the comb, it ripped out some of my baby hairs. I could see them knotted in the comb after she was finished. I'm not usually tender headed, but that hurt.

Disappointingly, I forgot to bring the coupon with me to my appointment, so I paid full price for this negative experience.<//Review><Pics>None< /Pics>< Response>

<Text>It's a gun shop..not a thrift store or a hardware store.. GUNS and ammo (if you buy a gun). I understand both the angst from customers and from the shop owners. These are sketchier times. As far as my runnings with the shop.. generally prickly at times and warmer customer service at other times.. just depends on the moment.  I have had excellent suggestions and have not been led astray for the sake of a sale. When something wasn't right about a purchase they took extra effort and even did some tactical repair work to make things right. I go back when the occasion arises. We don't have many options in San Francisco so just call before you go and get things clear about your intentions with the shop. Mins dumpling house is one of the better places to eat in the ie (assuming you like dumplings.) The reason for the 3 that I feel the menu could have more dumplings and less other dishes. I come here semi regularly, and unfortunately I am stuck ordering the same dishes every time.

The establishment is small, and very tidy!! This is a big plus.

While I only give Mins a 3, I do highly recommend it. If you've never had a juicy dumpling before, you're missing out!!!

Until next time...< /Review>< userid>
